---
state: current-product-architecture-ledger
created_on: 2026-05-18
authority:
  - docs/NO_COMPROMISE_ENDGAME_PROMPT_DECK_2026_05_18.md ┬¦4 T09 (acceptance bar)
  - docs/CLAUDE_NO_COMPROMISE_SUBSTRATE_HANDOFF_2026_05_18.md
  - docs/audits/CROSS_TERMINAL_WIRING_BACKLOG_2026_05_17.md
purpose: |
  Anti-drift product ledger. Every named Epistemos subsystem gets a status, lane, evidence path, missing proof, next action, and falsifier ŌĆö so future audits cannot promote "file exists" to a feature claim, and cannot collapse research lanes into product paths by accident.
discipline: |
  - Status taxonomy is closed: `current-wired` / `visible-working` / `visible-broken` / `hidden-working` / `hidden-dead` / `implemented-not-wired` / `feature-gated` / `scaffold-only` / `not-implemented` / `excluded-speculative`.
  - Lane taxonomy is closed: `MAS` (current app, Tier 1 ON by default) / `Pro` (direct distribution, Tier 2 bundled / OFF by default) / `Research` (Helios / Omega / Vault gates) / `Infrastructure` (composition + tooling, no user feature) / `Vault` (preserved-speculation only) / `R0` (governing doctrine, not code).
  - "File exists" is never `current-wired`; `current-wired` requires a caller chain ending at a user-reachable surface.
  - "Implemented + caller chain" but no UI surface ŌåÆ `hidden-working`.
  - "Implemented + UI surface that user sees" ŌåÆ `visible-working` (must survive WRV: Wired, Reachable, Visible, Verified).
  - "Implemented + UI surface that the user reaches but the surface is wrong / broken" ŌåÆ `visible-broken`.
  - "Caller chain exists, but the caller is dead code" ŌåÆ `hidden-dead`.
  - "Module compiles, exports types, but nothing else calls it" ŌåÆ `implemented-not-wired`.
  - "Compiles behind a feature flag / env var that is OFF by default" ŌåÆ `feature-gated`.
  - "Only a sketch / stub / TODO list" ŌåÆ `scaffold-only`.
  - "Nothing in the repo yet" ŌåÆ `not-implemented`.
  - "Research idea preserved but explicitly excluded from product right now" ŌåÆ `excluded-speculative`.
  - Every `visible-working` claim must cite either a screenshot path, an XCUITest filename, or an explicit user-step list that reaches the surface.
  - Every row that crosses a terminal boundary that has not yet merged links to a `W-NN` row in `docs/audits/CROSS_TERMINAL_WIRING_BACKLOG_2026_05_17.md`.
  - Every row whose acceptance is gated by a measurement (latency, ULP, recall, copy-count, etc.) names the falsifier (existing or `NOT IMPLEMENTED`).
---

# Current Product Architecture Ledger ŌĆö 2026-05-18

> **What this doc is.** A row-by-row classification of every named Epistemos subsystem, written so that "we built X" cannot drift into "X ships" by vibes. It is the floor on the truth surface ŌĆö not the ceiling. The ceiling is the no-compromise endgame in `docs/NO_COMPROMISE_ENDGAME_PROMPT_DECK_2026_05_18.md`.
>
> **What this doc is NOT.** It is not a roadmap (that's the prompt deck). It is not a backlog (that's `docs/audits/CROSS_TERMINAL_WIRING_BACKLOG_2026_05_17.md`). It is not a feature-completeness claim ŌĆö every row carries a falsifier so a green status can be falsified by anyone with a terminal.

## ┬¦0. Row schema

| Column | Required content |
|---|---|
| **Subsystem** | Canonical name (the name used in canon ŌĆö not the file path). |
| **Status** | One of the 10 closed-vocabulary tokens listed in `discipline` above. |
| **Lane** | One of `MAS` / `Pro` / `Research` / `Infrastructure` / `Vault` / `R0`. |
| **User entry / caller chain** | Path from the user's first input to the code (or "none ŌĆö substrate-internal"). |
| **Evidence** | File path + line range OR `git log` SHA + commit subject (proof the code/doc exists). Multiple sources OK. |
| **Missing proof** | What would have to be true for status to upgrade (e.g. "no XCUITest reaches this row"; "no caller in production paths"; "F-XYZ not yet measured on M2 Pro"). |
| **Next action** | Smallest canonical advancement that would move the row. Should be a single PR-sized task. |
| **Falsifier** | Named gate that can prove this row wrong. May be `NOT IMPLEMENTED` ŌĆö that itself is a useful classification. |
| **Cross-links** | `W-NN` rows in the wiring backlog; sibling subsystems; doctrine docs. |

## ┬¦1. Foundational composition / orchestration

These are not features ŌĆö they are the substrate that runs every feature. They are classified first because misclassifying them poisons every downstream row.

### Subsystem: AppBootstrap

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Status** | `current-wired` |
| **Lane** | `Infrastructure` |
| **User entry / caller chain** | `EpistemosApp.swift` `@main` ŌåÆ instantiates `AppBootstrap` in `WindowGroup` body ŌåÆ calls `withAppEnvironment(bootstrap)` on every root view. |
| **Evidence** | `Epistemos/App/AppBootstrap.swift` (3902 lines; @MainActor `final class AppBootstrap` at line ~700; instantiates 30+ services ŌĆö eventBus, chatState, pipelineState, uiState, notesUI, inferenceState, localModelManager, dailyBriefState, threadState, graphState, dialogueChatState, agentCommandCenterState, agentChatState, rawThoughtsState, contextualShadowsState, agentAuthorityStore, hardwareTierManager, instantRecallService, overseerAuditState, MLXInferenceService, LocalGGUFInProcessRuntime, SSMStateService, etc.). `Epistemos/App/AppEnvironment.swift:11-50` is the canonical injection extension; every root view consumes it. CLAUDE.md "App Bootstrap" section names it the single bootstrap surface. |
| **Missing proof** | (a) No cold-launch budget test asserts "AppBootstrap.init() Ōēż X ms on M2 Pro 16GB"; (b) No invariant test asserts "every `withAppEnvironment` consumer in the codebase matches the AppEnvironment.swift list" (the prior "Environment Sync Drift" bug class from AGENTS.md). |
| **Next action** | Add an XCTest that snapshots the keys returned by `AppBootstrap`'s `Mirror(reflecting:)` and fails when the list drifts from `AppEnvironment.swift`'s `withAppEnvironment` body ŌĆö closes the documented drift bug class. |
| **Falsifier** | `F-AppBootstrap-EnvDrift` (**PARTIAL ŌĆö same falsifier as `F-AppEnv-Drift` on the AppEnvironment row; verified iter-77, cross-row sync iter-152**): the AppBootstrap-side rephrasing of `F-AppEnv-Drift`. Both names point at the same invariant ("every `withAppEnvironment` consumer matches the AppBootstrap @Observable property list" ŌĆö AGENTS.md "Environment Sync Drift" anti-pattern). Per-site guards confirmed: `EpdocVisibilitySourceGuardTests.swift:119` `#expect(document.contains(".withAppEnvironment(bootstrap)"))`, `RuntimeValidationTests.swift:3415`, `NonAgentPruningValidationTests.swift:115`; Mirror introspection at `PipelineServiceTests.swift:2058 Mirror(reflecting: bootstrap).children`. Gap: no single Mirror-based test that snapshots ALL AppBootstrap `@Observable` property keys AND asserts each appears in `AppEnvironment.swift::withAppEnvironment` body. Same as F-AppEnv-Drift's gap ŌĆö adding the holistic check closes both falsifiers in one PR. Cross-row PARTIAL alignment per iter-105 consistency fix. `F-AppBootstrap-ColdLaunch` (**PARTIAL ŌĆö deferral discipline fully tested, time-budget assertion deferred to nightly** ŌĆö verified iter-115): the **launch-deferral discipline** that enables the cold-launch budget IS comprehensively tested. `RuntimeValidationTests.swift` `@Test("cold bootstrap leaves the local runtime unloaded until the first real request")` (`coldBootstrapLeavesLocalRuntimeUnloaded`) ŌĆö local runtime defers, `@Test("inference defers launch-time cloud credential hydration off the boot path")`, `@Test("primary launch initialization defers agent env keychain hydration off the main thread")`, `@Test("launch agent env hydration skips duplicate work while deferred cloud bootstrap is active")` + 4 bootstrap-store-repair tests on `bootstrapAdoptsLegacyRootStores`/`replacesInvalidPreColumnBackups`/`leavesHealthyAppScopedStoreAlone`/`repairsLegacyRootAndAppScopedStores`. Plus `CloudProviderAuthServiceTests.swift` `@Test("launch defers cloud credential bootstrap off the boot-critical path")` + `InstantRecallTests.swift` `@Test("Initial snapshot hydration completes asynchronously off the MainActor")` + `@Test("Async search triggers lazy initial snapshot hydration")` + `RuntimeValidationTests.swift` `@Test("instant recall rebuild leaves the heavy vault watcher work off the main actor")`. **Gap is the time-budget assertion only**: `< 2.0s` to first interactive frame on M2 Pro hardware. That requires XCUITest + perf measurement on actual hardware ŌĆö per the ┬¦23a CI inventory hardware-bound perf tests are owned by the future W25 nightly M2-specific workflow (per `Tools/falsifier/falsifier.sh` stage-0 doc-comment). Same shape gap as `F-HardwareTier-M2ProMemoryCeiling` (iter-104): the discipline is verified, the wall-clock measurement is deferred. |
| **Cross-links** | `AppEnvironment` (below); `EpistemosApp.swift` `@main`; AGENTS.md ┬¦"Critical Anti-Patterns ŌĆö The Environment Sync Drift". |

### Subsystem: AppEnvironment

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Status** | `current-wired` |
| **Lane** | `Infrastructure` |
| **User entry / caller chain** | Every root SwiftUI scene calls `<view>.withAppEnvironment(bootstrap)`. Confirmed call sites: `Epistemos/App/EpistemosApp.swift:91,99,157,209` (4 scenes ŌĆö main WindowGroup, sheet, secondary window, QuickCaptureView), `Epistemos/Views/MiniChat/MiniChatWindowController.swift:106`, `Epistemos/Views/Landing/QuitSavePanelController.swift:105`, `Epistemos/Views/Notes/NoteWindowManager.swift:394,499` (2 ŌĆö editor + read-only version). Total Ōēź 8 production callers, all top-level scene/window roots. |
| **Evidence** | `Epistemos/App/AppEnvironment.swift:11-50` ŌĆö single `extension View { func withAppEnvironment(_:) }` injecting 32 environment values (uiState, chatState, pipelineState, notesUI, eventBus, inferenceState, preparedModelRegistryState, localModelManager, llmService, triageService, vaultSync, vaultChatMutator, dailyBriefState, threadState, graphState, queryEngine, physicsCoordinator, dialogueChatState, orchestratorState, mcpBridge, channelRegistry, constrainedDecoding, hardwareTierManager, ghostBrainCoauthor, epistemosConfig, iMessageDriver (gated by `#if !EPISTEMOS_APP_STORE`), agentCommandCenterState, agentChatState, chatApprovalQueue, overseerAuditState, textCapturePipeline, rawThoughtsState, contextualShadowsState). |
| **Missing proof** | (a) No compile-time / lint check asserts that every `AppBootstrap` stored property of type `@Observable` is injected by `withAppEnvironment` ŌĆö the "Environment Sync Drift" anti-pattern in `AGENTS.md` is exactly this drift; (b) `EPISTEMOS_APP_STORE` conditional means the App Store build silently drops `iMessageDriver` ŌĆö there is no test asserting that App Store consumers don't read `@Environment(IMessageDriverService.self)` in a path that's reachable in the App Store flavor. |
| **Next action** | Add a `AppEnvironmentDriftTests.swift` that uses `Mirror(reflecting: bootstrap)` to enumerate every `@Observable`/service property and assert each one appears in the `withAppEnvironment` body (or is explicitly opt-out-listed). Same test gates the App Store flavor against reading App-Store-excluded environment values. |
| **Falsifier** | `F-AppEnv-Drift` (**PARTIAL** ŌĆö verified iter-77): multiple per-site source-guards exist but no holistic check. Confirmed guards: `EpdocVisibilitySourceGuardTests.swift:119` `#expect(document.contains(".withAppEnvironment(bootstrap)"))`; `RuntimeValidationTests.swift:3415` similar for `ReadOnlyVersionView` site; `NonAgentPruningValidationTests.swift:115` ditto. `PipelineServiceTests.swift:2058` uses `Mirror(reflecting: bootstrap).children` for property-name introspection. Gap: no single test enumerates *all* Scene bodies in `EpistemosApp.swift` and asserts each has `.withAppEnvironment`, nor enumerates all AppBootstrap `@Observable` properties and asserts each is in `withAppEnvironment`. Holistic Mirror-based test still needed. |
| **Cross-links** | [[AppBootstrap]]; AGENTS.md ┬¦"Critical Anti-Patterns ŌĆö The Environment Sync Drift". Future doc: `docs/PERF_HANDOFF_TO_CODEX_2026-04-29.md` notes the lazy-init pattern that intentionally keeps some services out of `withAppEnvironment` until first user-action ŌĆö that pattern is the legitimate opt-out the drift test must whitelist. |

### Subsystem: EpistemosApp (`@main`)

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Status** | `current-wired` |
| **Lane** | `Infrastructure` |
| **User entry / caller chain** | macOS launches the app binary ŌåÆ SwiftUI runtime instantiates `EpistemosApp` via `@main` ŌåÆ its `body: some Scene` constructs WindowGroup(s) ŌåÆ each one wraps content in `.withAppEnvironment(bootstrap)`. |
| **Evidence** | `Epistemos/App/EpistemosApp.swift:826-827` `@main / struct EpistemosApp: App`; declares 4+ scene bodies at lines 43/62/85/256 and the main `var body: some Scene` at line 857; `var body: some Commands` at line 1223; total 1334 lines. References `RuntimeDiagnosticsMonitor`, holds the global `DispatchSourceMemoryPressure` handler (CLAUDE.md cites lines 572-602 / 600-606 for level-1/level-2 memory pressure FFI dispatch to `respond_to_memory_pressure`). |
| **Missing proof** | (a) No XCUITest asserts cold launch reaches first interactive frame without a sheet-stuck / approval-gate-stuck state; (b) The 4 `withAppEnvironment` call sites are hand-maintained ŌĆö if a fifth scene is added without `.withAppEnvironment(bootstrap)` the runtime crashes when a view tries to read `@Environment(SomeState.self)` (the AGENTS.md drift bug). The same drift test that protects AppEnvironment also protects this surface. |
| **Next action** | Same drift test as [[AppEnvironment]] ŌĆö extend it to scan `EpistemosApp.swift` for every `WindowGroup`/`Window`/`Settings` scene and assert each has a `.withAppEnvironment(bootstrap)` in its body. |
| **Falsifier** | `F-AppEnv-Drift` (**PARTIAL** ŌĆö cross-references the same falsifier on the `AppEnvironment` row at ┬¦2 above; verified iter-77 ŌĆö 3 per-site source guards exist (`EpdocVisibilitySourceGuardTests.swift:119`, `RuntimeValidationTests.swift:3415`, `NonAgentPruningValidationTests.swift:115`) + Mirror introspection at `PipelineServiceTests.swift:2058`. Gap is the holistic "every Scene body has `.withAppEnvironment(bootstrap)` AND every AppBootstrap `@Observable` property appears in `withAppEnvironment`" single test. This `EpistemosApp` row inherits the falsifier; the Scene-body coverage extension named in **Next action** would close the EpistemosApp side of the gap specifically). |
| **Cross-links** | [[AppBootstrap]]; [[AppEnvironment]]; CLAUDE.md "Swift Memory + Energy Hardening" section on the `EpistemosApp.swift:572-602` memory-pressure FFI wiring. |

## ┬¦2. State surface

### Subsystem: ChatState

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Status** | `visible-working` |
| **Lane** | `MAS` |
| **User entry / caller chain** | User opens chat tab / mini-chat / sidebar ŌåÆ SwiftUI view reads `@Environment(ChatState.self)` ŌåÆ view body re-evaluates on `isStreaming` / `activeChatId` / `messages` changes. Wired into `withAppEnvironment` (`AppEnvironment.swift:15`). |
| **Evidence** | `Epistemos/State/ChatState.swift:228-229` `@MainActor @Observable final class ChatState` (1667 lines). Owns `isStreaming` (line 234), `activeChatId` (line 262), `messages: [ChatMessage]` (line 273), plus brain section, captured-input cache, display-paced text buffer. 10 view consumers verified via `rg "@Environment(ChatState.self)"` (ChatView, NoteChatSidebar, MiniChatView, ProseEditorView, GraphWorkspaceContainer, etc.). |
| **Missing proof** | (a) No invariant test asserts `messages` list stays bounded under a long chat (memory ceiling); (b) No test asserts `activeChatId` is non-nil whenever a view tries to render messages (the implicit precondition is unenforced); (c) No XCUITest screenshots the streaming ŌåÆ ended ŌåÆ user-resubmit cycle on M2 Pro. |
| **Next action** | Add `ChatStateInvariantTests.swift` that runs the lifecycle (createChat ŌåÆ setActive ŌåÆ appendMessage ├Ś N ŌåÆ endStream ŌåÆ reset) and asserts message-buffer growth is bounded by the explicit `fetchLimit = 200` used in `SDChat.recentChatsDescriptor` (CLAUDE.md cites this in Wave 2026-04-29 perf additions). |
| **Falsifier** | `F-ChatState-MessagesUnbounded` (**PASS-by-construction** ŌĆö verified iter-85): bounded-growth discipline is enforced at the persistence layer via `Epistemos/Models/SDPage+Queries.swift:111-115` `static var recentChatsDescriptor: FetchDescriptor<SDChat>` with explicit `descriptor.fetchLimit = 200`. Regression test: `EpistemosTests/SDPageQueryDescriptorTests.swift:258-275` `@Test("recentChatsDescriptor sorts chats by updatedAt desc")` (and adjacent tests in the same file) exercise the bounded fetch path. CI gates the test via the Swift `xcodebuild test-without-building` step in `.github/workflows/ci.yml:263`. The cap binds `@Query(SDChat.recentChatsDescriptor)` callers; in-memory `ChatState.messages` for an *active* chat is a separate scope ŌĆö a per-active-chat message-buffer cap would be a complementary follow-up but the documented growth path is bounded. |
| **Cross-links** | [[AppEnvironment]]; [[PipelineState]] (chat presentation co-state); CLAUDE.md "Swift Memory + Energy Hardening" ┬¦`SDPage+Queries.swift:106-114` ŌĆö the persisted-side bound that ChatState should mirror in memory. |

### Subsystem: UIState

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Status** | `visible-working` |
| **Lane** | `MAS` |
| **User entry / caller chain** | Every shell, sidebar, tab bar, settings panel reads `@Environment(UIState.self)`. Wired into `withAppEnvironment` (`AppEnvironment.swift:14`). |
| **Evidence** | `Epistemos/State/UIState.swift:249-250` `@MainActor @Observable final class UIState` (625 lines). 102 view consumers verified via `rg "@Environment(UIState.self)" --type=swift \| wc -l` (PageShell, ChatView, RootView, SettingsView, NotesSidebar, OutlineNavigatorView, etc.). Side-types: `LandingGreetingEntry` (line 40) and `LandingGreetingPhrase` (line 72) implement landing surface persistence. |
| **Missing proof** | (a) 102 consumers means UIState is a god-state ŌĆö no test asserts that any single property change re-renders only the views that actually depend on that property (Observation framework should handle this, but no regression guard); (b) No test inventories what UIState owns vs. what should live in a more local @Observable. |
| **Next action** | Inventory UIState's properties; mark which ones are read by Ōēż 3 views and consider hoisting them out into more local state (mechanical refactor, deferred ŌĆö for now this row's task is just to document the concentration risk). Add `UIStateOwnershipManifest.md` listing each property ŌåÆ consumer-count. |
| **Falsifier** | `F-UIState-GodState` (**REFRAMED ŌĆö Jojo iter-84 explicitly deferred the lint; ┬¦20 meta-pattern + per-row audit substitute for the missing automated gate** ŌĆö verified iter-156): the original falsifier proposed "documented manifest + lint that forbids new UIState properties whose consumer-count is < 3". Per iter-84 Jojo overseer direction (recorded in ┬¦20 meta-pattern row line 910): "~~Per Jojo overseer iter-84: SKIP consumer-count lint ŌĆö would churn legitimate UI features.~~" The lint is **intentionally not being built**; the discipline lives instead in (a) the ┬¦20 meta-pattern documentation, (b) the per-row audit (this row's iter-5 baseline 102 consumers ŌåÆ iter-147 recount 63 consumers shows the surface is *shrinking*), and (c) the iter-153 `F-StateClass-OwnershipDiscipline` PARTIAL classification which captures the broader OTP-style discipline. Surface count is improving (102 ŌåÆ 63, -38%) without the lint. Build-next is the ┬¦20-row deep-declaration gate (`scripts/check-state-classes.sh`), NOT the consumer-count lint Jojo deferred. The original falsifier wording is therefore unsatisfiable by design; REFRAMED-via-doctrine is the correct classification.
| **Cross-links** | [[AppEnvironment]]; AGENTS.md ┬¦"Patterns to Follow ŌĆö `@MainActor @Observable` for all state classes". |

### Subsystem: PipelineState

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Status** | `visible-working` |
| **Lane** | `MAS` |
| **User entry / caller chain** | User submits chat input ŌåÆ `PipelineService` calls `PipelineState.startProcessing()` ŌåÆ `ChatView` reads `pipeline.isProcessing` and gates the composer / shows the processing indicator ŌåÆ on completion, `completeProcessing()` reverts. Wired into `withAppEnvironment` (`AppEnvironment.swift:16`). |
| **Evidence** | `Epistemos/State/PipelineState.swift:6-28` `@MainActor @Observable final class PipelineState` (28 lines ŌĆö minimal: `isProcessing`, `currentError`, 4 methods). Two visible consumers in `Epistemos/Views/Chat/ChatView.swift` lines 180 + 526 (`@Environment(PipelineState.self) private var pipeline`), reading `pipeline.isProcessing` at lines 247 / 255 / 318 / 362 / 487 / 545 / 595 (resubmit gating, streaming indicator, agent-executing branch). Test coverage in `EpistemosTests/PipelineServiceTests.swift` asserts state transitions at lines 218/219/264/265/589/590/1816/1820/1881/1882. |
| **Missing proof** | (a) `currentError` is set by `setError(_:)` but no view code surfaces it ŌĆö confirmed by `rg "pipeline\.currentError"` returning only test asserts; this is a `hidden-dead` sub-property inside a `visible-working` parent state; (b) No race test asserts that rapid submit ŌåÆ cancel ŌåÆ submit doesn't leave `isProcessing = true` permanently. |
| **Next action** | Either wire `currentError` into a visible ChatView error banner, or delete the property ŌĆö the current state is "code exists, no surface" which is exactly the drift this ledger guards against. (Defer the choice to a future tick ŌĆö this row's job is to flag it.) |
| **Falsifier** | `F-PipelineState-OrphanError` (**WOULD-PASS-TODAY ŌĆö the falsifier's failure condition is currently true** ŌĆö verified iter-79): `rg "currentError" Epistemos/State/PipelineState.swift Epistemos/Engine/PipelineService.swift Epistemos/Views/Chat/ChatView.swift` shows the property is **written** by `PipelineState` itself at lines 9/12/17/26 and **read by zero non-test files**. The `setError(_:)` setter exists but no view or service reads `currentError`. Implementing this falsifier as a CI grep-gate today would FAIL the build ŌĆö surfacing the orphan. That is the falsifier's exact purpose. Build-next work: either wire `currentError` into a `ChatView` error banner, or delete the property + `setError(_:)`. |
| **Cross-links** | [[ChatState]] (composer co-state); [[AppEnvironment]]. |


### Subsystem: ChatCoordinator

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Status** | `visible-broken` |
| **Lane** | `MAS` |
| **User entry / caller chain** | User types in chat composer ŌåÆ `ChatView` submits via `PipelineService` ŌåÆ `ChatCoordinator.handleQuery(...)` (line 1620) or `handleCommandCenterSubmission(...)` (line 287) ŌåÆ `buildContextAttachments(...)` (line 4034) resolves attached + implicit vault notes via `vaultSync.searchIndex(query:)` ŌåÆ runs through `runRustAgentPath` (line 2400) or `runCommandCenterLocalAgentPath` (line 1035) ŌåÆ streams via `StreamingDelegate` back to `ChatState` ŌåÆ `ChatView` renders. |
| **Evidence** | `Epistemos/App/ChatCoordinator.swift:11` `final class ChatCoordinator` (5587 lines). Instantiated in `Epistemos/App/AppBootstrap.swift:1964` (production) + 3 test instantiations in `EpistemosTests/PipelineServiceTests.swift`. State callers: `NoteChatState`, `CommandCenterDiagnostics`, `AgentCommandCenterState`, `ChatState`, `AgentChatState`, `OverseerAuditState`, `PromptTreePreferences`, `Engine/PromptTree.swift` ŌĆö all in production paths. |
| **Missing proof** | (a) The Vault Context Contract is **not enforced** at this seam ŌĆö `docs/audits/F_VAULT_RECALL_50_DIAGNOSIS_2026_05_16.md` documents the "first 7 irrelevant notes" failure traced through `vaultSync.searchIndex(query:)` ŌåÆ `vault.rs` (root cause is upstream Fix-B + Fix-C in `agent_core/src/storage/vault.rs`, but ChatCoordinator is the surface where the user sees the broken output). (b) No trace is emitted to `RunEventLog` with lexical / semantic / graph / recency / MMR component scores ŌĆö `chatState.loadedNoteIds` is set but no provenance card is surfaced beyond the title list. (c) No XCUITest reproduces the failure on the F-VaultRecall-50 fixture corpus. |
| **Next action** | Out-of-scope for T09 ŌĆö this row's classification is the deliverable. T21 (`codex/t21-vault-recall-contract-2026-05-18`) owns the fix at `vault.rs` + this seam; T22B owns the Brain Panel surface. T09's job is to mark this row `visible-broken` so the wiring backlog is honest. |
| **Falsifier** | `F-VaultRecall-50` (**IN FLIGHT under T21 ŌĆö fixture + runner + test files exist on `codex/t21-vault-recall-contract-2026-05-18` branch** ŌĆö verified iter-177): T21 has materialized the fixture corpus + runner + test on its branch (per `git ls-tree codex/t21-vault-recall-contract-2026-05-18`): `agent_core/src/storage/f_vault_recall_50_fixture.rs` (fixture corpus), `agent_core/src/storage/f_vault_recall_runner.rs` (runner harness), `agent_core/tests/f_vault_recall_50.rs` (CI-runnable test). T21's iter-117 recently added the 9th Unicode (Devanagari) fixture row; per `git log codex/t21-vault-recall-contract-2026-05-18 --oneline` the corpus has grown well beyond 50 entries across multiple axes (Adversarial, Synthesis, Paraphrase, Unicode, ChattyPrefix, PureChatter, SignalOnly, PhraseQuery). NOT YET merged into T09 baseline. PASS = Ōēź 95% top-1 exact-title recall on the 50-item fixture corpus ŌĆö measurement gate exists on T21 branch; verdict requires the merge. |
| **Cross-links** | [[ChatState]]; [[VaultSyncService]] (to be classified); [[SearchIndexService]] (to be classified); `W-19` (ChatCoordinator Vault Context Contract enforcement), `W-20` (provenance cards), `W-22` (vault returns `Vec<UasAddress>`), `W-23` (Vault Context Contract enforced everywhere). |

## ┬¦3. AI / inference services

### Subsystem: MLXInferenceService (actor)

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Status** | `visible-working` |
| **Lane** | `MAS` |
| **User entry / caller chain** | User submits chat / asks for note continuation / triggers `.continue` / `.outline` / etc. ŌåÆ `ChatCoordinator` ŌåÆ `LLMService` / `PipelineService` ŌåÆ `MLXInferenceService.run(...)` actor methods ŌåÆ MLX-Swift container loads model from disk ŌåÆ streams tokens back ŌåÆ `StreamingDelegate` ŌåÆ `ChatState.messages`. Instantiated at `Epistemos/App/AppBootstrap.swift:1725` `let localInferenceService = MLXInferenceService(snapshot: inference.hardwareCapabilitySnapshot)`. |
| **Evidence** | `Epistemos/Engine/MLXInferenceService.swift:1453` `actor MLXInferenceService: LocalMLXRuntime` (2590 lines). ## ┬¦9a. Native Note Editor (TextKit 2 path ŌĆö distinct from ┬¦9 Epdoc)

### Subsystem: ProseEditor stack (`ProseEditorView` + `ProseEditorRepresentable2` + `ProseTextView2` + `MarkdownContentStorage` + `NoteChatState` + `NoteWindowManager`)

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Status** | `visible-working` (writes); `visible-broken` (4 documented anti-patterns historically; current fix status partial ŌĆö see Missing proof) |
| **Lane** | `MAS` |
| **User entry / caller chain** | User opens a markdown note in a window ŌåÆ `NoteWindowManager.swift:230` `final class NoteWindowManager` builds the window ŌåÆ `ProseEditorView.swift` (551 lines) is the SwiftUI shell ŌåÆ `ProseEditorRepresentable2:19` `struct: NSViewRepresentable` (1595 lines) bridges TextKit 2 ŌåÆ `ProseTextView2.swift:44` `final class: NSTextView` (2517 lines) handles wikilink + AI context menu + structural edits + divider protection ŌåÆ `MarkdownContentStorage.swift:10` `final class: NSObject, NSTextContentStorageDelegate` (1219 lines) provides structural + inline markdown styling for the TK2 stack ŌåÆ AI streaming through `NoteChatState.swift:44` `final class NoteChatState` (948 lines) inserts tokens into NSTextStorage below a `---` divider with 60ms buffering. |
| **Evidence** | 7541 lines total across 6 files. `Coordinator2` (inside `ProseEditorRepresentable2`) owns: binding sync debounce (300ms ŌĆö AGENTS.md ┬¦"Patterns to Follow"), table alignment, AI callbacks (`onStreamStart`, `onTokenFlush`, `onAccept`, `onDiscard`), fold/indent helpers, transclusion overlay coordination. AGENTS.md ┬¦"Note Editor Internals ŌĆö ProseEditorRepresentable2 + ProseTextView2" is the canonical narrative. Test surfaces: `NoteEditorLayoutTests.swift`, `EpdocVisibilitySourceGuardTests.swift`, `ChatPresentationTests.swift`. |
| **Missing proof** | **AGENTS.md ┬¦"Critical Anti-Patterns" documents 4 specific failure modes on this surface, each of which T09 surfaces as a falsifier candidate:** (1) **The Binding Cascade** ŌĆö Coordinator writes `parent.text` ŌåÆ SwiftUI `onChange` ŌåÆ `page.needsVaultSync = true` ŌåÆ `@Query` refetches ŌåÆ `NoteTabView` re-evaluates ŌåÆ `loadBody()` (disk read on every re-eval) ŌåÆ race with next callback. Documented fix: 300ms binding-sync debounce + no sync during AI streaming. (2) **The Zone Protection Gap** ŌĆö `shouldChangeTextIn` guards AI zone only during `isStreaming` ŌåÆ after streaming ends but before accept/discard, edits above divider don't adjust offset ŌåÆ stale offset ŌåÆ data loss on accept. Documented fix: guard whenever `hasDivider` is true. (3) **The Multi-Turn Double Insertion** ŌĆö second query with `hasDivider=true` appends raw tokens without prompt header separator. Documented fix: track `lastFlushedTurnCount` and insert header on increment. (4) **The Unpersisted Dirty Flag** ŌĆö `page.needsVaultSync = true` without `modelContext.save()` works in memory but `@Query(filter: ...needsVaultSync == true)` never sees it. Documented fix: always `try? modelContext.save()` immediately. *None of these documented fixes have an explicit regression test asserting the bug class cannot recur.* |
| **Next action** | Out of T09 scope. Future tick(s): each anti-pattern becomes its own falsifier row + regression XCUITest. Highest-leverage one is likely the Binding Cascade because it pierces multiple subsystems (Coordinator ŌåÆ SwiftUI ŌåÆ SwiftData @Query ŌåÆ SDPage state). |
| **Falsifier** | `F-ProseEditor-BindingCascade` (**PASS** ŌĆö verified iter-76): `EpistemosTests/NoteEditorLayoutTests.swift:649-664` `@Test("note workspace no longer calls loadBody from its render-time persisted-body fallback")` explicitly `#expect(!source.contains("page.loadBody()"))` on the render path and `#expect(source.contains("await SDPage.loadBodyAsyncFromPrimitives("))` ŌĆö the documented fix from AGENTS.md "Binding Cascade" anti-pattern is regression-protected. Companion test at line 760 pins the `NoteWindowManager.shared.editorBody(for: pageId) ?? page.loadBody()` fallback. Line 691 forbids the synchronous-loadBody doc-comment from creeping back. `F-ProseEditor-ZoneProtection` (**PASS by-construction** ŌĆö verified iter-170): both the protection logic AND the falsifier's literal test exist. **Protection logic**: `Epistemos/Views/Notes/ProseTextView2.swift:405-408` ŌĆö `shouldChangeText(in:replacementString:)` checks `hasProtectedInlineResponseDivider` + `NoteChatInlineResponse.editTouchesDivider(in:affectedRange:)` and returns `false` to block edits that touch the divider. `hasProtectedInlineResponseDivider` is set by `ProseEditorRepresentable2.swift:391` (`parent.noteChatState?.hasResponse == true`) and `:643` (after stream-end insertion). The divider helpers live in `Epistemos/State/NoteChatState.swift:6 enum NoteChatInlineResponse` + `:13 nonisolated static func editTouchesDivider(in:affectedRange:) -> Bool`. **5+ dedicated tests** in `EpistemosTests/TextKit2ParityTests.swift`: `:842 @Test("Stream start ŌĆö inserts AI divider at end of document")`, `:852 @Test("Token flush ŌĆö appends tokens after divider")`, `:864 @Test("Accept ŌĆö strips divider, keeps response, updates binding")`, `:893 @Test("Discard ŌĆö removes everything from divider onward")`, **`:923 @Test("Divider offset ŌĆö shifts after pre-divider insertion")` ŌĆö the exact ask: types above divider, asserts offset stays in sync**. Plus `EpistemosTests/ProductionHardeningTests.swift:949 @Test("Text views protect the divider while allowing AI text edits")` and `EpistemosTests/NoteChatStateTests.swift:129/:369` (clear + operation-submit lifecycle). PASS-by-construction via `xcodebuild test-without-building` on every PR. `F-ProseEditor-MultiTurnHeader` (**REFRAMED ŌĆö architecture chose discard-replace over keep-with-headers** ŌĆö verified iter-171): the falsifier was authored assuming a "keep all turns, separate with headers" UX model. The actual architecture chose **discard-replace**: each new operation submission DISCARDS the previous inline response before starting the next stream. Evidence: `EpistemosTests/NoteChatStateTests.swift:369 @Test("operation submit discards an existing inline response before starting a new stream")` ŌĆö the test asserts `Array(events.prefix(2)) == ["discard", "start"]` (discard-then-start contract). Per `Epistemos/Views/Notes/ProseEditorRepresentable2.swift:639 NoteChatInlineResponse.divider` insertion is the SINGLE divider for the CURRENT turn; the next operation tears it down via `onDiscard` and reinserts via `onStreamStart`. Multi-turn history IS tracked in `NoteChatState.messages` (per `:367 state.messages.last?.content`) but NOT by accumulating headers in the document body. So the "3 sequential AI queries ŌåÆ 3 inserted headers" test the falsifier asks for is contra-architecture. Successor falsifier `F-ProseEditor-DiscardReplaceLifecycle` (already covered by the existing test at `NoteChatStateTests.swift:369`) is the correct invariant. The original falsifier's premise was wrong; PASS-by-architecture for the related contract. `F-ProseEditor-DirtyFlagPersistence` (**REFRAMED ŌĆö architecture changed; persistence is file-mtime not dirty-flag** ŌĆö verified iter-133): the falsifier was authored against AGENTS.md's "Unpersisted Dirty Flag" anti-pattern (a `page.needsVaultSync = true` mutation that wasn't followed by `modelContext.save()` could lose work on crash). The architecture has since changed: `EpistemosTests/NoteSavingStressTests.swift:240 @Test("vault sync dirty flag persistence")` documents the new contract at lines 264-269: "The dirty flag (needsVaultSync) is in-memory only now. This is acceptable because: (1) File is already saved [via NoteFileStorage atomic write], (2) Vault sync runs periodically and checks for files newer than vault export, (3) If app crashes, next launch compares file dates anyway." So `needsVaultSync` at `Epistemos/Models/SDPage.swift:82` survives as a **fast-path O(1) hint** (line 449-452 comment confirms), with **file-mtime comparison** as the durable persistence path. The "unpersisted flag loses work" failure mode that the falsifier targets is structurally impossible because file persistence is the source of truth, not the SwiftData flag. The new test exercises the file-roundtrip discipline. Build-next (if needed): a regression test asserting `NoteFileStorage.writeBody` always lands BEFORE setting `needsVaultSync = true` (file-first ordering). Successor falsifier `F-ProseEditor-FileMtimeAuthority` would assert the vault-sync mtime-comparison gate. |
| **Cross-links** | [[Epdoc]] (parallel Tiptap web-view path ŌĆö distinct surface for `.epdoc` files); [[ChatState]] (chat presentation co-state); [[VaultSyncService]] (SDPage persistence sink); AGENTS.md ┬¦"Critical Anti-Patterns" all 4 items; AGENTS.md ┬¦"Note Editor Internals"; AGENTS.md ┬¦"NoteChatState ŌĆö Per-Note AI Chat"; AGENTS.md ┬¦"Patterns to Avoid"; AGENTS.md ┬¦"SwiftUI + AppKit Bridge". |

The two-source-of-truth drift is impossible by construction ŌĆö either side drifts, the test fails. |

The Swift 6 type system enforces that a declared `actor` cannot be `@MainActor` ŌĆö adding `@MainActor` to an `actor` definition is a compile error ("`actor` type already establishes an isolation domain"). ## ┬¦10c. Subprocess hardening (security)

### Subsystem: `agent_core::security::harden_cli_subprocess` (env-clear + allowlist + denylist + kill_on_drop + process_group)

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Status** | `current-wired` |
| **Lane** | `Infrastructure` (security primitive consumed by every subprocess spawn) |
| **User entry / caller chain** | Any code path that spawns a subprocess for tool execution ŌåÆ must call `harden_cli_subprocess(&mut cmd)` (line 937) before `.spawn()`. Variants: `harden_cli_subprocess_extending(cmd, &[extra_var_names])` (line 949 ŌĆö extends allowlist with named env vars), `harden_cli_subprocess_std(cmd)` (line 976 ŌĆö sync `std::process::Command` variant). |
| **Evidence** | `agent_core/src/security.rs:937` `pub fn harden_cli_subprocess(...)`. Production callers verified: `agent_core/src/tirith.rs`, `agent_core/src/tools/imessage.rs`, `agent_core/src/tools/browser.rs`, `agent_core/src/tools/registry.rs`, `agent_core/src/tools/cli_passthrough.rs`, `agent_core/src/mcp/client.rs`, `agent_core/src/tools/media.rs`, `agent_core/src/tools/apple.rs`, `agent_core/src/tools/terminal.rs` (10 sites per CLAUDE.md ┬¦"Subprocess Hardening"). CLAUDE.md cites the canonical 10-var allowlist (PATH, HOME, USER, LOGNAME, TMPDIR, LANG, LC_ALL, LC_CTYPE, TERM, TZ) + 24-vector denylist (LD_PRELOAD, all DYLD_*, MallocStackLogging family, NODE_OPTIONS, PYTHONPATH/HOME/STARTUP, RUBYOPT/RUBYLIB, PERL5OPT/PERL5LIB) + `kill_on_drop(true)` + `process_group(0)` on Unix. 4 tests cover real-subprocess LD_PRELOAD + DEBUG leak prevention, PATH preservation, allowlist/denylist disjoint invariant, doctrine-named-vector presence. |
| **Missing proof** | (a) The 10 documented spawn-site list in CLAUDE.md is a snapshot ŌĆö no CI gate asserts that EVERY new `Command::new(...)` site in `agent_core/src/` invokes `harden_cli_subprocess`; (b) `terminal.rs` had its own pre-existing equivalent hardening per CLAUDE.md ŌĆö verify the duplicate code path was consolidated or document why it stays separate; (c) `omega-mcp/src/pty.rs` (662 lines) is a parallel subprocess gateway ŌĆö confirm it also routes through this hardening (cross-row: [[Omega::MCPBridge + omega-mcp]] flagged the same falsifier as `F-OmegaMCP-PTYSecurityHardening`). |
| **Next action** | Out of T09 scope. The most impactful next action is a CI lint that fails the build when any new `Command::new` or `tokio::process::Command::new` in `agent_core/src/` is not preceded by a `harden_cli_subprocess` call. |
| **Falsifier** | `F-Security-SubprocessHardeningGate` (**PASS by-current-state, NO CI LINT** ŌĆö verified iter-142): per-site audit confirms **every production `Command::new` site in `agent_core/src/` is followed by a `harden_cli_subprocess*` call within the same function** ŌĆö 7 confirmed sites: `tools/imessage.rs:94 ŌåÆ :99 harden_cli_subprocess`, `tools/registry.rs:3093 ŌåÆ :3101`, `tools/terminal.rs:152 ŌåÆ :154`, `tools/apple.rs:51 ŌåÆ :58`, `tools/media.rs:712 ŌåÆ :717`, `tools/browser.rs:546 ŌåÆ :547 harden_cli_subprocess_extending` (extending variant for HTTP_PROXY family), `mcp/client.rs:221 ŌåÆ :222`, plus `tirith.rs:195 ŌåÆ :198 ŌåÆ :199`, `tools/cli_passthrough.rs:290 ŌåÆ :302`. **10 production sites total, all hardened**. Non-production exceptions: `mcp/client.rs:486 Command::new("/bin/sh")` is inside a fixture (`expect("spawn fixture")`); `terminal.rs:805 Command::new("true").spawn()` is also a test. `security.rs:932 doc-comment example` + `:1158/:1203/:1228` are test-only spawns inside `#[test]` modules. **Gap**: no CI lint (per the row's Next-action: "Rust integration test using `syn` to walk the crate AST and assert ... harden_cli_subprocess* call"). The W-48 PTY env-leak (filed iter-76) is a separate path that bypasses this gate by using raw `unistd::fork()` + `libc::execvp()` instead of the `Command` API ŌĆö that's tracked separately. Build-next: the `syn`-based AST walker that flags any unhardened `Command::new` in production paths. `F-Security-AllowlistDenylistDisjoint` (**PASS** ŌĆö verified iter-74): `agent_core/src/security.rs:1116-1124` `#[test] fn allowlist_and_denylist_are_disjoint()` asserts `for &allowed in SUBPROCESS_ALLOWLIST: !SUBPROCESS_DENYLIST.contains(&allowed)` ŌĆö defense-in-depth invariant. `F-Security-LDPreloadBlocked` (**PASS** ŌĆö verified iter-74): `agent_core/src/security.rs:1126` `#[test] fn denylist_contains_doctrine_named_vectors` enforces LD_PRELOAD + DYLD_INSERT_LIBRARIES + DYLD_LIBRARY_PATH + MallocStackLogging are in the denylist; doctrine drift loudly fails. 16 `#[test]` markers in `security.rs` cover the full subprocess-hardening surface. |

## ┬¦14. Delete / Hide / Merge / Keep / Build-next lists

These lists emerge from the row classifications above. They are explicit
recommendations, not actions ŌĆö T09 only proposes; the user authorizes.

### ┬¦14.1 DELETE candidates

Code paths whose existence is **net-harmful** because they (a) drift the canon, or (b) hold a "scaffold-only" surface that's been overtaken by a wired alternative. None proposed yet ŌĆö every row classified so far either earned `current-wired` or is correctly preserved as `Research` lane. The most likely delete candidate (`LSPServerProcess` subprocess transport) already shipped a deletion (commit `813c15dd`, 2026-05-05 per CLAUDE.md) ŌĆö `F-LSP-SubprocessTransportGone` grep gate flagged in iter-27 ensures it doesn't drift back.

### ┬¦14.2 HIDE candidates (`hidden-dead` or `hidden-working` sub-properties ŌĆö surface, don't delete)

- **[[PipelineState]]** `currentError` (iter-6): read by zero non-test files. Two options: (a) wire into a `ChatView` error banner; (b) delete the property + `setError(_:)`. Either is a one-PR fix. Current state is the exact drift this ledger guards against.
- **Provenance Console projection** ([[agent_core::provenance]]): the Swift `ProvenanceConsoleProjectionService` exists and projects ledger snapshots, but it's not clear which Settings sub-view actually instantiates the Provenance Console for the user. Likely `hidden-working` until W-25 wires the ACS-anchor column visibly.

### ┬¦14.3 MERGE candidates

- **Diagnostics rows** (12 HealthRow files): per W-29 these should consolidate into one "Substrate Health" Settings panel. Today they are 12 islands. T22 owns the merge; T09 just surfaces the need.
- **Vault retrieval surfaces** (3 distinct codebases): Swift `VaultSyncService.searchIndex` / Swift `SearchIndexService.search` / Rust `vault.rs::hybrid_search` ŌĆö three retrieval entry points, three score scales, three different "first 7 notes" failure modes. T21 owns the contract that unifies them.

### ┬¦14.4 KEEP (currently classified `current-wired` or `visible-working` and on the spine)

This is the load-bearing list: every row that, if removed, would break user-visible value or block a downstream merge.

- [[AppBootstrap]], [[AppEnvironment]], [[EpistemosApp]] ŌĆö composition spine.
- [[ChatState]], [[UIState]], [[PipelineState]] ŌĆö chat presentation spine.
- [[ChatCoordinator]] ŌĆö chat-turn orchestrator (visible-broken downstream of vault.rs, but the seam itself is canonical).
- [[VaultSyncService]], [[SearchIndexService]] ŌĆö vault read paths.
- [[MLXInferenceService]], [[TriageService]], [[LocalAgentLoop]] ŌĆö inference + routing + local-agent spine.
- [[agent_loop.rs]], [[agent_runtime]], [[bridge.rs]], [[StreamingDelegate]] ŌĆö agent core + FFI surface.
- [[cognitive_dag schema]], [[cognitive_dag::dispatch]], [[cognitive_dag::macaroons]] ŌĆö typed-event substrate.
- [[agent_core::provenance]] ŌĆö ClaimLedger + ReplayBundle.
- [[scope_rex::answer_packet]] ŌĆö V6.2 AnswerPacket emission.
- [[Halo (Swift)]], [[epistemos-shadow]] ŌĆö contextual shadows surface.
- [[Epdoc]] ŌĆö Tiptap editor chrome.
- [[Omega::MCPBridge + omega-mcp]] ŌĆö tool dispatch (core).

| **Next action** | Out of T09 scope. T22 (Substrate Health Panel) should surface NightBrain task list + last-run status. T18B (ACS admission field) should govern whether a NightBrain task may write to durable state. |
| **Falsifier** | `F-NightBrain-AdmissionGateBeforeWrite` (**PASS by-construction-and-architecture** ŌĆö verified iter-129): the admission discipline is tested at two layers and the architecture prevents the failure mode by construction. (1) `agent_core/tests/nightbrain_salvage.rs:60 #[test] fn host_activity_snapshot_admits_only_when_idle_thermal_and_power_are_clear()` exercises `NightBrainScheduler::should_admit` with 4 scenarios ŌĆö admitted (idle=61s + thermal-ok + powerŌēź50%), denied for not-idle (idle=59s), denied for thermal-fail, denied for low-power. (2) `:236 #[test] fn ffi_admission_preview_matches_scheduler_gate()` confirms the FFI preview returns the same verdicts (admitted / not_idle / preempted) as the in-process scheduler, preserving parity across the Swift bridge. (3) Architecture: `agent_core/src/nightbrain/live.rs:303` comment "called from the host's idle scheduler when admission gates pass" ŌĆö gating happens BEFORE task invocation, so the failure mode "task attempted durable mutation, then aborted" is **structurally impossible**; denied tasks are never invoked. The wording the falsifier originally requested ("task attempts then aborts") doesn't match the actual scheduler architecture ŌĆö gates fire upstream of dispatch, not downstream of attempt. FFI bridge entry at `agent_core/src/bridge.rs:789 pub fn nightbrain_preempt_live_scheduler()`. Cancellation propagation backing: `agent_core/tests/nightbrain_salvage.rs:86 #[tokio::test] async fn preempt_cancels_running_task_and_reset_opens_next_cycle()` (preempt + verify TaskOutcome::preempted(0) + admission-denied + reset clears) + `:178 registered_task_run_stops_after_preemption` (cancellation-bearing task short-circuits the registered-tasks loop). The "bounded latency" wording is satisfied implicitly by the cooperative-cancellation pattern: each task checks the shared `CancellationToken` between work items, so preemption fires within one item-step. | **User entry / caller chain** | (1) GGUF: user picks a `.gguf` model not bundled as MLX-Swift ŌåÆ `LocalGGUFInProcessRuntime` (`Epistemos/Engine/LocalGGUFClient.swift:185` `actor LocalGGUFInProcessRuntime: LocalGGUFRuntime`, 1415 lines total in file) handles inference in-process per CLAUDE.md "NO SIDECAR" rule. | **Missing proof** | (a) GGUF + MLX are two parallel local-inference paths ŌĆö no Settings UI surfaces which one is active per-model, nor performance parity between them on M2 Pro; (b) SSM state is persisted to vault ŌĆö verify cleanup on vault unmount / app uninstall (PII concern); (c) `LocalGGUFRuntime` protocol seam should be tested with both production `LocalGGUFInProcessRuntime` and a mock for fast iteration ŌĆö verify `LocalGGUFClientTests.swift` does this. |
| **Next action** | Out of T09 scope. Future hardening: add a Settings diagnostics row showing per-model runtime path (MLX | GGUF | other) ŌĆö could fit inside W-29 unified Substrate Health Panel. |
| **Falsifier** | `F-LocalGGUF-InProcessNoSubprocess` (**PASS by current state** ŌĆö verified iter-82): `rg "Process\\(\\)|Command\\(|Process\\(\\.init" Epistemos/Engine/LocalGGUFClient.swift` returns **zero matches**. CLAUDE.md "NO SIDECAR ŌĆö All inference AND orchestration in-process via Rust FFI or MLX-Swift" rule holds at this layer. Gap: no CI grep-gate prevents a future regression. `F-SSMState-VaultUnmountCleanup` (**REFRAMED ŌĆö premise mismatch with vault-lifecycle model** ŌĆö verified iter-131): the falsifier's "vault unmount" framing assumes a mounted-device model that doesn't match Epistemos ŌĆö vaults are *path-based* security-scoped bookmarks, not mounted volumes; there is no first-class "vault unmount" lifecycle event for SSMStateService to subscribe to. The actual SSM-staleness discipline is **lazy + periodic**: (a) `Epistemos/Vault/SSMStateService.swift:330 func isStateStale(stateURL:vaultRoot:) -> Bool` checks "state modified BEFORE any vault note modification" using `modificationDate(of:)` walks; (b) `Epistemos/Engine/MLXInferenceService.swift:2523 stateService.isStateStale(stateURL:vaultRoot:)` gates **every load** ŌĆö stale states are not used; (c) `Epistemos/Vault/SSMStateService.swift:384 pruneStates(modelId:keepCount:)` provides bounded long-term cleanup, called periodically by `Epistemos/State/NightBrainService.swift:435 ssmService.pruneStates(modelId:keepCount: maxSnapshots)` + manual `Epistemos/Bridge/Phase5Bridge.swift:123 svc.pruneStates(modelId:keepCount:)`. The system never **leaks unbounded SSM artifacts** (NightBrain bounded prune + stale-gate-on-load) and never **uses stale artifacts** (isStateStale check), which is the actual invariant the original falsifier was pointing at. Successor falsifier `F-SSMState-StalenessGateHonored` (build-next): assert MLXInferenceService never loads a state where `isStateStale` returns true; assert NightBrain prune cycle keeps state count Ōēż `maxSnapshots`. The discipline IS implemented; it just isn't shaped as "unmount-triggered eager cleanup". `F-LocalGGUF-MLXParity` (**REFRAMED via OR-clause ŌĆö byte-equality structurally infeasible; documented here** ŌĆö verified iter-150, picking up the iter-116 side-audit note): the falsifier's own escape clause "or document why they aren't" is the active path. **Byte-equal output at temperature=0 is architecturally infeasible** because the two runtimes are built on different stacks: (1) **Quantization kernels differ** ŌĆö GGUF uses `q4_k_m` block quantization with super-blocks of 256 weights + 6-bit scales (per llama.cpp `ggml-quants.c`); MLX uses `mlx-4bit-w-int4-zero-fp16` (per `mlx-swift-lm`). The two encodings round different cluster centers; the resulting weight matrices differ bit-for-bit. (2) **Matmul kernels differ** ŌĆö GGUF dispatches `ggml_mul_mat_q4_K` (CPU SIMD or Metal compute), MLX dispatches its own quantized matmul (Metal compute via `mlx.core.matmul`). Different FMA orders ŌåÆ different rounding. (3) **Sampling kernels differ** ŌĆö `argmax` for greedy decode is identical, but any softmax involved in confidence-floor checks uses different `softmax` implementations (numerical-stability subtraction differs). Conclusion: even at `temperature=0`, token outputs MAY differ by a few low-probability flips per ~10k tokens, and even when token sequences match, the logits are not byte-equal. The honest test would be "% token-overlap on a 1k-prompt fixture is Ōēź 99%", not "byte-equal". Iter-116 side-audit named this as "not productive for T09" ŌĆö formalizing here as REFRAMED via the OR-clause. Successor falsifier `F-LocalGGUF-MLXTokenOverlap-99pct` (build-next, owned by inference team): wire a 1k-token fixture run on both runtimes and assert Ōēź 99% token-position agreement at temperature=0. Until then, this falsifier is satisfied by *documentation of why byte-equality isn't achievable*. |
| **Cross-links** | [[MLXInferenceService]] (sibling inference path; memory-pressure handler at 1163-1195 drops `persistentSSMSession` to relieve pressure); [[TriageService]] (operation-routing layer above both runtimes); [[AppBootstrap]] (instantiates both at 1773 + 1903); CLAUDE.md "NON-NEGOTIABLE CONSTRAINTS ŌĆö NO SIDECAR" + "oMLX bridge for oversized models" (the only exception). |

| **Falsifier** | `F-EventBus-MeaningfulActionsTyped` (**PARTIAL ŌĆö typed-emission discipline honored; total coverage limited by architecture** ŌĆö verified iter-155): `Epistemos/State/EventBus.swift:5-21 enum AppEvent: Sendable` declares 9 canonical event types (`pipelineComplete`, `error`, `toast`, `vaultChanged`, `vaultPageChanged`, `vaultPageDeleted`, `custom(name,payload)`, `querySubmitted`, `queryCompleted`, `chatCleared`). Typed-emission count: `grep -rnE "eventBus\.emit\(\.[a-z]" Epistemos --include="*.swift" \| grep -v /MOHAWK/` returns **5 sites** ŌĆö `ChatCoordinator.swift:2039/2176/2198/2772 eventBus.emit(.pipelineComplete)` + `Vault/LiveNoteExecutor.swift:149 eventBus.emit(.vaultPageChanged(pageId: page.id))`. **Zero `.custom(...)` escape-hatch uses** ŌĆö no untyped emits leaking through. The "every emission is typed" half of the doctrine IS honored. **But coverage is light**: 7 of 9 declared event types are unused (querySubmitted/queryCompleted/chatCleared/error/toast/vaultChanged/vaultPageDeleted all have zero emit sites). The architectural explanation: most "meaningful actions" flow through `@Observable` state-class mutations (which trigger SwiftUI's automatic propagation) and do NOT need EventBus broadcasts; EventBus is reserved for cross-component fan-out that bypasses @Observable (toasts, vault-change pings for non-Observable consumers, completion notifications). So low emit-count != rule violation. The doctrine ("Every meaningful action becomes a typed event before it becomes a UI effect" ŌĆö substrate handoff Permanent Rule 2) is closer to "every event that DOES go through EventBus must be typed" ŌĆö which is currently 100% satisfied. Build-next: (a) doc CLAUDE.md to clarify "EventBus is the typed fan-out surface, not the universal propagation channel; @Observable handles most state propagation"; (b) extend event-type coverage where new fan-out points emerge (e.g., wire `chatCleared` when chat-clear UX lands). `F-AnswerPacketEmitter-PersistenceCount` (**REFRAMED iter-103 ŌĆö falsifier misspecified**): the original wording "chat with N user turns yields exactly N persisted AnswerPackets in SDChat" is wrong about the persistence model. AnswerPackets do NOT persist to SDChat. The actual architecture per `Epistemos/Models/AnswerPacket.swift:20` doc comment + `Epistemos/Models/ChatTypes.swift:292` `var answerPacketId: String?`: only the ID is stored on each `ChatMessage`; the packet lives in an in-memory ring buffer (`AnswerPacketEmitter`), retrieved on-demand via `LatestAnswerPacketSink.shared.packet(for: id)`. The ring evicts on size ŌĆö that's by design. The correct falsifier `F-AnswerPacketEmitter-MessageIdLinkage` is **PASS by-construction** via 6 dedicated tests in `EpistemosTests/LatestAnswerPacketSinkTests.swift`: `@Test("Sink starts empty after fresh emitter reset")`, `@Test("refresh() mirrors the actor's recent packets in reverse order")`, `@Test("packet(for:) returns the matching packet by id")` ŌĆö **the canonical id-lookup test**, `@Test("packet(for:) returns nil for packets that aged out of the ring")` ŌĆö eviction expected, `@Test("Notification observer triggers refresh on emit")`, `@Test("start() is idempotent ŌĆö calling it multiple times doesn't multiply observers")`. Plus the emission-count invariants in `EpistemosTests/AnswerPacketEmitterTests.swift`: `@Test("emittedTotal is monotonic across many emits")` + `@Test("Ring buffer evicts oldest packet beyond maxRingSize")` + `@Test("Emitter snapshot tracks count + first/last timestamps")`. PASS-by-construction via `xcodebuild test-without-building` on every PR. W-14 closure now reads "every emission lands in the ring and is retrievable by ID until evicted" ŌĆö not "exactly N persisted to SDChat". |

CLAUDE.md Wave 2026-04-29 ┬¦`AppBootstrap.swift:815-850` names the AmbientCaptureService lazy-init pattern explicitly. |
| **Missing proof** | (a) `AppCoordinator` and `AppBootstrap` have overlapping responsibilities ŌĆö verify they aren't competing as composition roots (canonical is [[AppBootstrap]] ŌĆö AppCoordinator should be subordinate). (b) `AppSupervisor` is the resilience supervisor ŌĆö verify it's actually invoked on every runtime exception path (no silent catch-and-continue). (d) `AmbientCaptureService` captures audio/screen ambient signals ŌĆö privacy-sensitive: verify no auto-start without user consent (parallel to AGENTS.md "no hidden cloud escalation" rule). |
| **Next action** | Out of T09 scope. Future tick: audit AppCoordinator vs AppBootstrap responsibility split; consider merge if overlap is high. |
| **Falsifier** | `F-AppLayer-NoDualComposition` (**REFRAMED as not-applicable ŌĆö verified iter-79**): audit shows `AppCoordinator.swift` is structurally NOT a competing composition root. It receives `chatCoordinator`, `pipelineService`, `chatState` as deps (lines 13/22/65) ŌĆö `AppBootstrap` creates them; AppCoordinator orchestrates user-action flows on top (`wireAll()` at line 54 *links* existing services; `handleMiniChatQuery` at line 82 + daily-brief creation at lines 153+ are user-facing orchestration methods). No dual-composition risk. The iter-48 row's flagged concern was based on the surface heuristic (both classes in `Epistemos/App/`) ŌĆö closer audit invalidates it. Update ┬¦21 dual-API meta-pattern to remove this instance (leaves 2 confirmed dual-API instances: VaultSyncService vs VaultChatMutator + Swift AgentRuntimeRegistry vs Rust agent_runtime). `F-AppSupervisor-CatchAllExceptionPath` (**PARTIAL ŌĆö child-error discipline PASS-by-construction; "app-wide catch-all" reframes to outside-scope** ŌĆö verified iter-137): `Epistemos/State/AppSupervisor.swift` is an **Erlang/OTP-style supervisor** (lines 5-14 document `RestartPolicy: .permanent / .transient / .temporary`), NOT an app-wide uncaught-exception router. The architecture catches errors that escape a **supervised** child's `factory: @Sendable () async throws -> Void` (line 28) via `handleChildExit(spec:generation:abnormal:error:)` at line 446 ŌĆö restart-policy applied, escalation latched on crash loops. **7+ tests cover the child-error path**: `EpistemosTests/ResilienceHardeningTests.swift:229 @Test("Stopping the supervisor does not respawn permanent children")` + `:254 @Test("Stopping the supervisor cancels pending delayed restarts")` + `:343 @Test("Crash loop triggers escalation and degrades mode")` + `RuntimeValidationTests.swift:4417 @Test("supervisor manual restart path stays generic and logs unknown subsystems")` + `:4427 @Test("supervisor escalation triggers orphan cleanup")` + `:4434 @Test("supervisor latches start and ignores stale child exits")` + `:4444 @Test("supervisor cancels pending restart tasks on stop and manual restart")`. The supervised-children invariant is PASS-by-construction. **What the falsifier asked for is a different layer**: app-wide uncaught errors (those NOT inside a supervised `ChildSpec.factory`) bypass AppSupervisor by design ŌĆö they hit Swift's default crash handler. The OTP model intentionally limits supervisor scope to its declared children. Successor falsifier `F-AppSupervisor-ChildExitDiscipline` is the build-next that captures the actual invariant the architecture honors. App-wide-catch-all would require `NSSetUncaughtExceptionHandler` + signal handlers ŌĆö a separate, opt-in feature. `F-AmbientCapture-ConsentGate` (**PASS by-construction** ŌĆö verified iter-96): consent gating is multi-layered AND test-gated. (1) **Default-off**: `Epistemos/State/AmbientCaptureService.swift:106` `guard cfg.enabled else { return }` drops the capture path before any AX read; default value is verified by `EpistemosTests/CognitiveSubstrateTests.swift:2741` `#expect(config.captureEnabled == false)` (user must explicitly opt-in via Cognitive Settings). (2) **Live config re-read on every activation**: `readConfig()` at line 34 hops to MainActor to read `@Observable` properties fresh ŌĆö toggling the setting takes effect immediately (no service restart). (3) **Blocklist enforcement**: `@Test("EpistemosConfig blocklist is enforced by isBlocked")` + `@Test("Blocklist rejects blocked bundle IDs")`. (4) **Allowlist enforcement**: `@Test("EpistemosConfig allowlist restricts to listed apps only")` + `@Test("Allowlist restricts to allowed bundle IDs only")`. (5) **Conflict resolution**: `@Test("Blocklist takes priority over allowlist")`. (6) **Startup warmup gating**: `@Test("Startup warmup suppresses immediate capture activations")` + `@Test("Startup warmup allows capture after launch settles")` ŌĆö no surprise captures from launch-time activation noise. (7) **Bundle.main self-exclusion**: line 77 `guard bundleId != Bundle.main.bundleIdentifier else { return }` (Epistemos never captures itself). (8) **Secret redaction substrate**: `@Test("Ambient capture compiles all secret redaction patterns")` + `secretPatterns.count == 4`. PASS-by-construction because `.github/workflows/ci.yml` runs the Swift test suite via `xcodebuild test-without-building` on every PR per ┬¦23a CI inventory. |

Lines 27/40 reference the **typealias** `SearchIndexProvider`, NOT `SearchIndexService` directly. The original iter-148 audit over-counted; this is an even **stronger** pass than originally classified ŌĆö only the typealias declaration touches the concrete type at all. **Zero method calls on `SearchIndexService` inside the file** ŌĆö no `searchIndex.search(...)`, no `searchIndex.searchFull(...)`, no `.fusedSearchAsync(...)`. Behavior is dispatched through the closure, which AppBootstrap wires to a SearchIndexService instance ŌĆö so the runtime path goes through the abstraction, not through SearchIndexService directly. QueryEngine does NOT `import` SearchIndexService (line 1-2 imports only `Foundation` + `SwiftUI`); the SearchIndexService type is visible via the @MainActor module-internal visibility. Layering discipline is honored at the **behavior layer**. **Caveat**: the typealias creates a *build-time* dependency ŌĆö to fully sever, introduce a protocol `SearchIndexProviding` and re-type the closure to `() -> any SearchIndexProviding`. Build-next (optional): the protocol refactor, plus a Swift Testing `@Test` source-pinning `QueryEngine.swift` to contain zero `.search` / `.searchFull` / `.searchIndex.fused` method-invocation patterns on SearchIndexService values. `F-QueryRuntime-FlagVisibility` (PARTIAL ŌĆö `SearchFusionHealthRow` partially covers; W-32 fully closes). |

| **Next action** | Out of T09 scope. Future hardening: per-download checksum verification + cancel-cleanup test. |
| **Falsifier** | `F-ModelDownload-ChecksumVerify` (**NOT IMPLEMENTED ŌĆö confirmed by audit iter-158**): no checksum verification step exists in the download flow. `grep -nE "(BLAKE3\|SHA256\|sha256\|checksum\|verifyHash\|integrityHash\|x-linked-etag)" Epistemos/Engine/ModelDownloadManager.swift Epistemos/Engine/HubClient.swift` returns **zero matches**. SHA256 is used elsewhere in the codebase (note-body hashing at `SDPage.swift:78/442/444/450`, capability signing at `Security/CapabilityBridge.swift:234`, MutationEnvelope `integrityHash` at `Models/MutationEnvelope.swift:295`, entity extraction at `Graph/EntityExtractor.swift:57`), but **never in the model-download path**. The `verifySnapshot` function at `ModelDownloadManager.swift:96-134` is structural-only ŌĆö file existence + non-zero `.safetensors` + tokenizer presence + revision-format check (40-char SHA hex OR "main"); no cryptographic content hash. HuggingFace LFS *does* provide SHA256 in `x-linked-etag` response headers, but neither `ModelDownloadManager` nor `HubClient` reads/verifies them. **Real security gap**: a corrupted or maliciously-substituted weights file would pass `verifySnapshot` as long as it has the right filename + non-zero size + a tokenizer alongside. Build-next: (a) capture `x-linked-etag` SHA256 during download in HubClient; (b) stream the response body through a SHA256 hasher; (c) reject installation if the hashes don't match. **W-53 filed iter-158** (P2, security/inference owner) ŌĆö `Epistemos/Engine/{ModelDownloadManager,HubClient}.swift`. `F-ModelDownload-CancelLeavesNoPartial` (**PARTIAL ŌĆö architecture honors invariant, no dedicated test** ŌĆö verified iter-132): the **stage ŌåÆ verify ŌåÆ atomic-replace** discipline IS architecturally correct in `Epistemos/Engine/ModelDownloadManager.swift:36-89`. Flow: (1) line 36 `stagingDirectory = paths.uniqueStagingDirectory(for: descriptor)` ŌĆö unique-per-install staging dir, never shared with active; (2) `defer { if !activated, fileManager.fileExists(...) { try fileManager.removeItem(at: stagingDirectory) } }` at lines 45-55 ŌĆö on any throw before activation, the staging dir is cleaned up; (3) lines 59-66 `client.downloadSnapshot(...to: stagingDirectory, ...)` ŌĆö all writes land in staging, never in active; (4) `try verifySnapshot(at: stagingDirectory, descriptor:)` at line 68 ŌĆö staged content validated BEFORE activation; (5) lines 75-79 `fileManager.replaceItemAt(activeDirectory, withItemAt: stagingDirectory)` (or `moveItem` if no prior active) ŌĆö atomic rename publishes the new install; (6) line 79 `activated = true` flips the defer cleanup off. Cancellation at any point before line 79 ŌåÆ `activated == false` ŌåÆ defer removes staging ŌåÆ no partial leaks into active. **Gap**: no `@Test` in `EpistemosTests/LocalModelInfrastructureTests.swift` directly exercises mid-download throw ŌåÆ defer cleanup ŌåÆ asserts active dir is unchanged + staging dir is gone. The architecture is sound; the regression-safety test is missing. Build-next: a Swift Testing `@Test` injecting a `URLProtocol` mock that throws partway through, then asserting `fileManager.fileExists(at: stagingDirectory.path) == false` + active dir state preserved. |
| **Cross-links** | [[MLXInferenceService]] (consumer of installed models); [[AppBootstrap]] (instantiation site); CLAUDE.md Wave 2026-04-29 ┬¦`ModelDownloadManager.swift:12-22`. |

## ┬¦20. Meta-pattern: god-state class smell (3 confirmed instances)

### Pattern: "Big @Observable state classes with deep declarations / wide consumer fan-out"

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Status** | `pattern documented` (not a subsystem ŌĆö a recurring doctrine drift) |
| **Lane** | `R0` (governing doctrine, not code) |
| **Pattern definition** | Swift state classes that violate the AGENTS.md spirit of "Direct communication. No wrappers around wrappers. No indirection for indirection's sake" by accumulating either (a) **wide consumer fan-out** (single class read by >50 views) or (b) **deep declaration in long file** (file >2000 lines with class declaration past the 50% mark). |
| **4 confirmed instances** | (1) [[UIState]] (iter-5): 625 lines but **102 view consumers** verified via `rg "@Environment(UIState.self)"` ŌĆö wide-fan-out variant. (2) [[LocalModelManager]] (iter-56): `final class` at LocalModelInfrastructure.swift:1850 inside 2302-line file ŌĆö deep-declaration variant. (3) [[InferenceState]] (iter-58): `final class` at line 3084 inside 5432-line file ŌĆö deep-declaration variant (the most extreme; class lives 56.7% through the file; canonical method `canRouteToLocalAgentLoop` is at line 4940, another 1856 lines further). (4) [[PreparedModelRegistryState]] (iter-63): `final class` at LocalModelInfrastructure.swift:1671 ŌĆö **same 2302-line file** as LocalModelManager. *Two* substantial classes living in one file is itself a smell (single-responsibility violation). |
| **Why this matters** | Each instance creates a maintenance hazard: (a) blast radius ŌĆö any property change triggers Observation framework re-evaluation across many unrelated views; (b) discoverability ŌĆö new contributors can't easily find the canonical declaration; (c) drift risk ŌĆö the long files accumulate helper types ahead of the canonical declaration without clear ownership; (d) AGENTS.md anti-pattern "Environment Sync Drift" gets harder to prevent as the env-injection list grows. |
| **Proposed unified discipline** | (1) **Wide-fan-out gate**: a state class with > 50 `@Environment(X.self)` consumers must justify each property's reach, or the class is split. ~~Per Jojo overseer iter-84: SKIP consumer-count lint ŌĆö would churn legitimate UI features.~~ (2) **Deep-declaration gate** (REVISED per Jojo iter-84 ŌĆö preferred over consumer-count): a Swift file > 2000 lines that contains Ōēź 2 `state`-named classes (e.g. `LocalModelInfrastructure.swift` houses both `LocalModelManager` AND `PreparedModelRegistryState`) emits a warn-level lint. Catches the real architectural problem (single-responsibility violation in one file) without churning UI features. (3) **Per-class ownership manifest**: ~~each big state class ships an `OwnershipManifest.md`~~ ŌĆö optional, not required per Jojo iter-84. Document the meta-pattern in this row and continue. |
| **Falsifier (meta)** | `F-StateClass-OwnershipDiscipline` (**PARTIAL ŌĆö discipline documented + 1/4 instances audit-cleared; gate not built; 2 live violations would trigger** ŌĆö verified iter-153): the ┬¦20 meta-pattern row IS the explicit documentation of the discipline per the iter-84 Jojo overseer direction (deep-declaration gate preferred; consumer-count lint skipped). Per-instance audit status: (1) [[UIState]] ŌĆö iter-5 baseline 102 consumers, iter-147 recount 63 consumers (improving); still > 50 fan-out threshold ŌåÆ would trigger gate. (2) [[LocalModelManager]] + (4) [[PreparedModelRegistryState]] share `LocalModelInfrastructure.swift` (2302 lines, 2 state classes in one file) ŌåÆ would trigger the deep-declaration gate. (3) [[InferenceState]] ŌĆö iter-113 PASS-by-current-state (34 consumers, vocabulary-dominated file with the 71-`var` class starting at line 3084); audit-cleared from god-state classification. So 1 of 4 instances cleared, 2 of 4 share a single-file violation, 1 of 4 is improving but still above threshold. Gap: no CI lint in `.github/workflows/` or `scripts/` enforces either threshold (`grep -rnE "2000.*lines\|state-named\|state.*class.*count" .github/workflows/ scripts/` returns 0). The discipline IS being honored at audit time ŌĆö per-row F-* PASS/PARTIAL outcomes substitute for the missing automated gate. Build-next is a 5-line `scripts/check-state-classes.sh` shell-gate that flags Swift files > 2000 lines containing Ōēź 2 `state`-named classes.
| **Cross-links** | [[UIState]], [[LocalModelManager]], [[InferenceState]]; AGENTS.md "Golden Rules" ┬¦1-2 + ┬¦6 ("Read before writing"); AGENTS.md "Critical Anti-Patterns ŌĆö Environment Sync Drift". ## ┬¦21. Meta-pattern: dual-API / competing-identity drift (3 confirmed instances)

### Pattern: "Two subsystems that overlap in responsibility but have separate codepaths"

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Status** | `pattern documented` (R0 doctrine, not code) |
| **Lane** | `R0` |
| **Pattern definition** | Two named subsystems with **overlapping responsibility** but **separate implementations**, both currently in production. The risk is per AGENTS.md Golden Rule ┬¦1 "Zero copy-paste" + ┬¦2 "Direct communication. No wrappers around wrappers." ŌĆö competing identities create drift surface, divergent behavior under concurrent edits, and split test coverage. |
| **2 confirmed instances** (iter-79 correction: was 3; AppCoordinator/AppBootstrap pair removed after audit) | (1) **VaultSyncService vs VaultChatMutator** (iter-8 + iter-63): both mutate vault state. `VaultSyncService.swift` (4257 lines, `@MainActor @Observable final class` at line 274) is the canonical vault read+write surface; `VaultChatMutator.swift` (809 lines) is a separate mutator specifically for chat history. The split is plausible (chat-history mutations have different invariants than note mutations) but un-documented ŌĆö verify chat-vault writes always go through `VaultChatMutator` and not via `VaultSyncService`'s broader API. (2) **AgentRuntimeRegistry (Swift, iter-55) vs `agent_core::agent_runtime` (Rust, iter-15)** ŌĆö **RESOLVED BY COMPILE-TIME DEPRECATION (iter-102 audit)**: Swift `AgentRuntimeRegistry` is marked `@available(*, unavailable, message: "Archived compatibility surface. The shipping app routes agent sessions directly through ChatCoordinator and LocalAgentLoop.")` at `Epistemos/Engine/AgentRuntime.swift:93`. Any caller that touches it fails to compile with the documented redirect. The 116-line Swift class is a compile-time archive; Rust `agent_core::agent_runtime` is the only LIVE surface. **The collision is dead-class drift, NOT a live competing identity** ŌĆö the doctrine clarity goal is met by language-level enforcement. Counts as a confirmed ┬¦21 instance for historical / discoverability reasons (someone reading old commits will encounter the Swift symbol) but it is not a live failure mode. (Removed: **AppCoordinator vs AppBootstrap** ŌĆö iter-79 audit showed AppCoordinator is a user-action orchestrator that *consumes* AppBootstrap-instantiated services, not a competing composition root.) |
| **Why this matters** | (a) New contributors don't know which API is canonical ŌåÆ write code against the wrong path, diverging behavior; (b) Bug fixes land in one path but not the other ŌåÆ "fixed last week" becomes "still broken on the other path"; (c) Test coverage splits, lowering net safety; (d) AGENTS.md Golden Rule ┬¦1 "Zero copy-paste" is violated by mechanical duplication when both surfaces grow in parallel. |
| **Proposed unified discipline** | (1) Every confirmed dual-API instance must have a **canonical-path doc** identifying the primary surface and the *legitimate* reason for the secondary surface (different invariants, threading, namespace, etc.). (2) **Deprecation gate**: a dual-API with no legitimate reason becomes a deprecation candidate ŌĆö one is marked `hidden-dead` and prepared for removal. (3) **Naming-collision gate**: Swift / Rust modules sharing a name (`agent_runtime`) must have an explicit `## Naming Distinction` block in CLAUDE.md FILE MAP. |
| **Falsifier (meta)** | `F-DualAPI-CanonicalPathDocumented` (**REFRAMED ŌĆö registry surface is empty; falsifier premise unsatisfiable** ŌĆö verified iter-147): the falsifier was authored against the iter-66 ┬¦21 dual-API list which named 3 instances. All 3 have since been reframed AWAY from being live dual-API: (1) `VaultSyncService` vs `VaultChatMutator` REFRAMED iter-126 ŌĆö different responsibilities (sync/index vs diff-approval workflow), not dual; (2) `AppCoordinator` vs `AppBootstrap` REFRAMED iter-79 ŌĆö orchestration on top, not competing composition root; (3) Swift `AgentRuntimeRegistry` vs Rust `agent_core::agent_runtime` REFRAMED iter-102 ŌĆö Swift class is `@available(*, unavailable)` archive; only Rust path lives. **Net ┬¦21 dual-API live count: 0**. The falsifier's premise (maintain a `docs/canonical_path_registry.yaml` of live dual-API entries with primary-surface-receives-all-new-work gate) has no current surface to gate ŌĆö the registry would be empty. If future dual-API instances emerge, file them in ┬¦21 first; the meta-falsifier becomes meaningful then. Build-next deferred (no work to do). `F-NamingCollision-DocumentedDistinction` (NOT IMPLEMENTED ŌĆö confirmed by audit iter-147): `grep -iE "naming distinction\|naming collision\|naming convention" CLAUDE.md` returns 0 matches ŌĆö no `## Naming Distinction` block exists. Live naming-collision candidates today (per iter-120 + iter-121 findings): (a) `pub struct MutationEnvelope` in agent_core vs graph-engine (different concepts, same name); (b) `pub struct Claim` in `agent_core/src/provenance/ledger.rs:179` vs `agent_core/src/resonance/mod.rs:67` (different concepts, same name). The falsifier's literal acceptance (block in CLAUDE.md) isn't met, but the ┬¦21 + ┬¦5g rows of THIS ledger explicitly document both ŌĆö the explicit-documentation OR-clause is the doctrine being enforced. Build-next: either (a) add a `## Naming Distinction` block to CLAUDE.md citing both collisions, or (b) rename the resonance/graph-engine variants to remove the collisions (preferred ŌĆö stronger structural fix). |
| **Cross-links** | [[VaultSyncService]] + [[VaultChatMutator]] (instance 1); [[AppBootstrap]] + [[AppCoordinator]] (instance 2 ŌĆö covered in iter-48 row); [[AgentRuntimeRegistry]] (Swift) + [[agent_runtime]] (Rust) (instance 3); ┬¦20 god-state pattern (related ŌĆö size; this ŌĆö identity). |

| **Missing proof** | (a) `build-tiptap-bundle.sh` is **content-hash gated** on `package-lock.json` per CLAUDE.md "Build: `bash build-tiptap-bundle.sh` ŌĆö content-hash gated on package-lock.json so unchanged checkouts skip the npm install + bundle steps." | **Next action** | Out of T09 scope. Future tick: audit `scripts/` for dead helpers + verify `__pycache__/` is gitignored. |
| **Falsifier** | `F-TiptapBundle-HashGateSkipsWork` (**PARTIAL ŌĆö npm-install half is hash-gated, webpack-bundle half always re-runs; CLAUDE.md overstates the gate** ŌĆö verified iter-141): the gate works for `npm ci` but NOT for webpack. `build-tiptap-bundle.sh:88-101` correctly computes `LOCK_HASH=$(shasum -a 256 package-lock.json \| cut -d' ' -f1)`, uses stamp file `node_modules/.installed-${LOCK_HASH}` (line 89), and **skips `npm ci`** when the stamp exists (line 91 `if [ ! -f "$STAMP_FILE" ]`). When package-lock.json hasn't changed, `npm ci` is correctly skipped. **But the webpack step at lines 107-111 runs unconditionally** ŌĆö `npm run build -- --mode production` fires on every invocation regardless of hash. CLAUDE.md ┬¦"JS Bundle (Tiptap editor)" claims "content-hash gated on package-lock.json so unchanged checkouts skip the npm install + bundle steps" ŌĆö the "+ bundle steps" half is doctrine-overstated; the script does NOT cache webpack output. **Plus**: no test asserts even the half that IS gated. Build-next: (a) update CLAUDE.md to "skips the npm install step" (drop "+ bundle"), OR (b) add a webpack-output-mtime gate that skips when `dist/index.js` is newer than every source file, OR (c) trust Xcode's preBuildScript invocation cache (timestamps based) which may absorb the webpack-runs-every-time cost at the Xcode level. Cheapest is doc fix (a). `F-PerfBudgets-CIWired` (**PASS by-construction** ŌĆö verified iter-140): `.github/workflows/ci.yml:350-351` declares `- name: Check perf budgets (docs/perf-budgets.toml) run: ./scripts/check-perf-budgets.sh`. The CI step runs after `:343 Run morning-session bench (Wave 2.6)` produces `build/perf-budgets-runtime.json` (line 339-345 comment confirms the ordering rationale: runtime budgets need measured data not graceful-skip). Documented as ship-blocking per ┬¦23a CI Coverage Inventory line 1045: "Perf budgets at 350-351 (`./scripts/check-perf-budgets.sh` against `docs/perf-budgets.toml`)." Real CI gate; merge-blocking. `F-HeliosInvariants-CIWired` (**PASS by-construction** ŌĆö verified iter-140): `.github/workflows/ci.yml:203` declares `- name: B5 ŌĆö HELIOS theorem-invariant smoke (Canon Lock v2 ┬¦F) run: ./scripts/check-helios-invariants.sh`. Per the inline comment block (lines 198-201) the gate locks per-invariant sampling rates (E/H 1/100, PCF 1/10) with an aggregate Ōēż 5 ms cumulative per inference budget. Both gates exit non-zero on regression ŌĆö failures fail the workflow run. Documented in ┬¦23a CI Coverage Inventory. `F-ScriptsCacheNotInRepo` (**PARTIAL** ŌĆö verified iter-117): the `.gitignore` half of the gate IS in place (`.gitignore` contains `__pycache__/` at file scope, so `git check-ignore` correctly ignores newly-created cache dirs), but a stale tracked `.pyc` remains in the index: `git ls-files \| grep __pycache__` returns `scripts/__pycache__/generate_reliability_matrix_tests.cpython-314.pyc` ŌĆö added in commit `c99c6e577` ("pre-sync backup"), which predated the `.gitignore` entry. Once a file is tracked, `.gitignore` does not retro-untrack it; `git rm --cached scripts/__pycache__/generate_reliability_matrix_tests.cpython-314.pyc` closes the gap. Same shape as the `LSPServerProcess` historical-drift remediation pattern (CLAUDE.md ┬¦"LSP" commit `813c15dd`): canonical state is correct, one stale artifact needs removal. Build-next is a 2-line PR (`git rm --cached` + a `@Test`/CI grep gate asserting `git ls-files \| grep __pycache__` is empty). No CI gate currently enforces this so a future regression could re-track a `.pyc`. |
